<h4 class="pt-cv-title"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%B6%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%AE%E0%A5%80%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%AA%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%A1%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%A4_%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%AE%E0%A5%81%E0%A4%A6%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%AF_%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%BE_%E2%80%98%E0%A4%B9%E0%A5%87%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%A5_%E0%A4%AE%E0%A4%B9%E0%A5%8B%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%B5_%E0%A4%86%E0%A4%B8%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A5%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%A6%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B6%E0%A4%A8_%E0%A4%94%E0%A4%B0_%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%B8%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%95%E0%A5%83%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%95_%E0%A4%A8%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%85%E0%A4%A6%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B5%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%80%E0%A4%AF_%E0%A4%AA%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B5"></span><a href="https://knowledgesthali.com/herath-festival-of-kashmiri-pandit-community/" class="_self" target="_self" >कश्मीरी पंडित समुदाय का ‘हेरथ’ महोत्सव: आस्था, दर्शन और सांस्कृतिक निरंतरता का अद्वितीय पर्व</a><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>

<h4 class="pt-cv-title"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="%E0%A4%AD%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%A4_%E0%A4%95%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%AA%E0%A4%B9%E0%A4%B2%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%9C%E0%A4%B2%E0%A4%AE%E0%A4%97%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A8_%E0%A4%A6%E0%A5%8B%E0%A4%B9%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%9F%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%AF%E0%A5%82%E0%A4%AC_%E0%A4%B5%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B2%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%A1%E0%A4%BC%E0%A4%95_%E0%A4%B8%E0%A5%81%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%97_%E0%A4%AC%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%B9%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%AE%E0%A4%AA%E0%A5%81%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B0_%E0%A4%95%E0%A5%87_%E0%A4%A8%E0%A5%80%E0%A4%9A%E0%A5%87_%E0%A4%B5%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%A4_%E0%A4%B9%E0%A5%8B%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%A8%E0%A4%AF%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%AD%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%A4"></span><a href="https://knowledgesthali.com/india-first-underwater-twin-tube-road-tunnel/" class="_self" target="_self" >भारत की पहली जलमग्न दोहरी ट्यूब वाली सड़क सुरंग: ब्रह्मपुत्र के नीचे विकसित होता नया भारत</a><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>
<div class="pt-cv-content">भारत की अवसंरचना (इन्फ्रास्ट्रक्चर) यात्रा में एक ऐतिहासिक अध्याय जुड़ने जा रहा है। केंद्र सरकार ने असम में ब्रह्मपुत्र नदी ...<br /><div class="pt-cv-rmwrap"><a href="https://knowledgesthali.com/india-first-underwater-twin-tube-road-tunnel/" class="_self pt-cv-readmore btn btn-success" target="_self">Read More</a></div></div></div>

<h4 class="pt-cv-title"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="%E0%A4%85%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%AE_%E0%A4%AE%E0%A5%87%E0%A4%82_%E0%A4%AA%E0%A5%82%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%B5%E0%A5%8B%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%B0_%E0%A4%AD%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%A4_%E0%A4%95%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%AA%E0%A4%B9%E0%A4%B2%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%87%E0%A4%AE%E0%A4%B0%E0%A4%9C%E0%A5%87%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%B8%E0%A5%80_%E0%A4%B2%E0%A5%88%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%A1%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%82%E0%A4%97_%E0%A4%AB%E0%A5%88%E0%A4%B8%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%B2%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%9F%E0%A5%80_ELF"></span><a href="https://knowledgesthali.com/northeast-india-first-emergency-landing-facility-in-assam/" class="_self" target="_self" >असम में पूर्वोत्तर भारत की पहली इमरजेंसी लैंडिंग फैसिलिटी (ELF)</a><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>
